[30;1m105 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m106 | [0m[35mShapely functions generally support multithreading by releasing the Global[0m
[30;1m107 | [0m[35mInterpreter Lock (GIL) during execution. Normally in Python, the GIL prevents[0m
[30;1m108 | [0m[35mmultiple threads from computing at the same time. Shapely functions[0m
[30;1m109 | [0m[35minternally release this constraint so that the heavy lifting done by GEOS can[0m
[30;1m110 | [0m[35mbe done in parallel, from a single Python process.[0m
[30;1m111 | [0m[35m[0m
